<div class="panel-region-separator"></div><div class="panel-pane pane-node-title"  id="page_title">
  
  
  
  <div class="pane-content">
    Privately Funded Programs  </div>

  
  </div>
<div class="panel-region-separator"></div><div class="panel-pane pane-node-body"  id="secondary_page_main">
  
  
  
  <div class="pane-content">
    <div id="internal_menu"><p style="text-align: right;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><a href="/what-we-do" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #6f1820; text-decoration: none; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.5em; text-align: right; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: bold; background: transparent;">WHAT WE DO</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span style="color: #333333;"><span style="border-style: initial; border-color: initial; line-height: 1.5em; background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-size: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial;">PRIVATELY FUNDED PROGRAMS</span></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a href="/academic-chairs" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #6f1820; text-decoration: none; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.5em; text-align: right; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: bold; background: transparent;">ISAS CHAIRS</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a href="/collaborators-partnerships" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #6f1820; text-decoration: none; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.5em; text-align: right; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: bold; background: transparent;">PARTNERSHIPS</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a href="committees" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #6f1820; text-decoration: none; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.5em; text-align: right; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: bold; background: transparent;">COMMITTEES</a></strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;">&nbsp;|&nbsp;</strong><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; background: transparent;"><a href="/isas-news" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 11px; vertical-align: baseline; color: #6f1820; text-decoration: none; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.5em; text-align: right; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: bold; background: transparent;">IN THE NEWS</a></strong></p></div><p><strong> </strong></p> <hr><p>ISAS has successfully secured private and government funds to enhance South Asia studies at Berkeley.</p><p style="text-align: center;"><img src="http://vcro-vm-i002-dev08.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/shared/Kundan10red1.jpg" width="125" height="155" style="float: right; border: 10px solid white;"></p><p><strong><a href="amrit-kaur-ahluwalia-memorial-grant-program">Amrit Kaur Ahluwalia Memorial Grant Program</a></strong></p> <p>ISAS  established the Amrit Kaur Ahluwalia Memorial Grant Program in 2000  with the generous support of Dr. Joginder Singh Ahluwalia and family. By  annually providing grants for summer research to select graduate  students, this program gives young scholars the opportunity to pursue  their first serious research in Sikh Studies.</p> <p><strong><a href="berkeley-bangla-initiative">Berkeley Bangla Initiative</a></strong></p> <p>This   initiative was started in 2003 to promote the study of Bangla language   and culture at UC Berkeley, as well as for the training of scholars,   development experts, and NGO activists to conduct research in and about   West Bengal and Bangladesh. UC Berkeley now teaches first and second   year Bangla, as well as other classes on the history and culture of   Bengal.</p><p><strong><a href="http://chowdhurycenter.berkeley.edu/" target="_blank">Subir and Malini Chowdhury Center for Bangladesh Studies</a></strong></p><p>The ISAS has received a major gift from the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subir_Chowdhury" target="_blank">Subir and Malini Chowdhury Foundation</a> to establish the Subir &amp; Malini Chowdhury Center for Bangladesh Studies. In  addition to promoting and integrating interdisciplinary scholarship,  the Subir and Malini Chowdhury Center will sponsor lectures and conferences.</p><p><a href="http://southasia.berkeley.edu/berkeley-pakistan-initiative-0" target="_blank"><strong>The Mahomedali Habib Distinguished Lecture Series on Pakistan</strong></a></p><p>The  Mahomedali Habib Distinguished Lecture Series on Pakistan is named in  honor of one of the leading figures in the history of the Habib family.  In addition to successfully guiding the Habib family’s transition from  India to Pakistan following independence in 1947, Mahomedali Habib laid  the foundations for the House of Habib, a group of powerful business  and financial companies. The group has a long-standing history of  philanthropy and social service and is currently leading the  establishment of Habib University, a liberal arts and sciences  university, in Pakistan which aims to bridge the gap between global  academia and Pakistan. Toward honoring the legacy of Mahomedali Habib  – who was distinguished by his love for Pakistan and his deep  commitment to education and philanthropy – the Habib family has decided  to endow an annual lecture series in his name. Through this lecture  series the Habib family aims to improve and diversify conversations  about Pakistan in the United States as well as create opportunities for  US and Pakistan-based scholars to dialogue. Our inaugural lecture was delivered by leading Pakistani lawyer, advocate of the Supreme Court  of Pakistan, President Supreme Court Bar Association of Pakistan and  human rights activist, <strong><a href="http://events.berkeley.edu/index.php/calendar/sn/csas.html?event_ID=68244&amp;date=2013-10-08&amp;filter=Target/Open%20To%20Audiences&amp;filtersel=" target="_blank">Asma Jahangir</a> </strong>on Tuesday, October 8, 2013. Details about this lecture <a href="http://events.berkeley.edu/index.php/calendar/sn/csas.html?event_ID=68244&amp;date=2013-10-08&amp;filter=Target/Open%20To%20Audiences&amp;filtersel=" target="_blank">here</a>.</p><p><strong><a href="telugu-studies-initiative">Berkeley Telugu Initiative</a></strong></p> <p>The   Berkeley Telugu Initiative aims to make Berkeley, and by extension,  the  Bay Area, a premier site for the cultivation and development of  Telugu  literature, humanities, performance and social science outside  of India.  With generous gifts from the community, a beginner level  Telugu  language course was launched in UC Berkeley in Fall 2007 as a  first step  of this initiative.</p> <p><strong><a href="sites/default/files/Bhandari.pdf">Bhandari Program on Indian Entrepreneurship in the Silicon Valley</a></strong></p> <p>The  Bhandari Program on Indian Entrepreneurship in the Silicon Valley was  launched in Fall 2007 with a new, yearlong course titled “The Indian  Diaspora in the Silicon Valley.” The goal of this course is to document  the achievements of the Indian entrepreneurs who have contributed  significantly to the rise of the Silicon Valley, and have helped  establish the region as a critical node in the global economy. This  program has been established with generous support from the Bhandari  Foundation, a charitable trust founded in 1994 by Narpat and Chandra  Bhandari of Los Gatos, California.</p> <p><strong><a href="http://www.lib.berkeley.edu/SSEAL/echoes/chapter6/chapter6_6.html">Gobind Behari Lal Scholarship in Science Journalism</a></strong></p> <p>In  1982, Phyllis Herron donated $5,000 to the UC Berkeley Graduate School  of Journalism upon her husband John Herron’s death. The gift was given  with the intention of creating a scholarship in memory of the Herron’s  long-time friend, Gobind Behari Lal, a science writer who won the  Pulitzer Prize in 1937 and the Padma Bhushan in 1969. Thereafter, Indian  community members donated additional funds to create a $10,000  endowment to support modest annual scholarships in science journalism  for deserving students in the Graduate School of Journalism. Currently,  the principle of the scholarship is $21,000, generating scholarships of  several hundred dollars for two or three students per year.</p> <p><a href="annual-lecture-series" target="_blank"><strong>Indo-American Community Lectureship in India Studies</strong></a></p> <p>This  Lectureship enables ISAS to bring prominent individuals from India to  Berkeley to deliver a lecture and interact with campus and community  members during a two-week stay. The Lectureship brings a scholar from  India every other year, and the Indian Council for Cultural Relations  (ICCR) pays the visitor’s international airfare. Past Lectureship  holders include Upendra Baxi, Andre Beteille, Madhav Gadgil, Ramachandra  Guha, Meenakshi Mukherjee, Narendra Panjwani, Anuradha Kapur, Ashis Nandy, and Amita Baviskar. With  the endowment exceeding $150,000, ISAS and ICCR agreed to make the  lectureship an annual occurrence.</p><p><a href="maharaj-kaul-memorial-fund" target="_blank"><strong>The Maharaj Kaul Memorial Fund</strong></a></p><p>Established  in  2010 in memory of Maharaj Kaul (1940 - 2009), a UC Berkeley  alum,  tireless  campaigner against injustice and for peace, founder of  groups  such as  India Relief and Education Fund, and Coalition Against  Communalism, and  long-time supporter of ISAS’s mission and activities,  the purpose of the Maharaj Kaul Memorial Fund is to provide support for   graduate fellowships and an annual lecture series on the  theme of  social justice through the&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px; background-color: #ffffff;">Institute</span>&nbsp;for South Asia  Studies at the  University of California, Berkeley. The inaugural Maharaj Kaul Memorial  Lecture was delivered by<a href="http://events.berkeley.edu/index.php/calendar/sn/csas.html?event_ID=41122&amp;date=2011-04-11&amp;filter=Target/Open%20To%20Audiences&amp;filtersel=" target="_blank"> Palagummi Sainath<strong>.</strong></a> More details <a href="maharaj-kaul-memorial-fund" target="_blank">here</a>. The second Maharaj Kaul Lecturer was Aruna Roy.</p> <p><strong><a href="http://buddhiststudies.berkeley.edu/awards/">The Padmanabh S. Jaini Graduate Student Award in Buddhist Studies</a></strong></p> <p>The  Padmanabh S. Jaini Graduate Student Award in Buddhist Studies was  established in 2009 with a generous gift from Professor Jaini that was  matched by the Chancellor's Matching Gift Program This award supports  high-achieving graduate students in Buddhist Studies at UC Berkeley and  honors Professor Jaini's important legacy in the field of Buddhist  Studies at UC Berkeley and beyond. Padmanabh S. Jaini is Professor  emeritus of Buddhist Studies and co-founder of the Group in Buddhist  Studies. For a list of past recipients of the Jaini Award, please click <a href="http://buddhiststudies.berkeley.edu/awards/jaini_award_recipients.html" target="_blank">here</a>.</p> <p><strong><a href="fellowships-grants-offered-csas">Qayum Family Foundation Grants for Travel and Conferences</a></strong></p> <p>The  Qayum Family Foundation Grants for Travel and Conferences was  established when the Qayum Family Foundation committed $5,000 annually  to fund a series of lectures and graduate fellowships through ISAS. This  pledge represents the first U.S. initiative on the part of the Qayum  Charitable and Educational Foundation, whose mission prioritizes support  of “secular principles of toleration, equitable progress, and unity in  India and the Indian diaspora.” The Foundation funds scholarships for  meritorious students, particularly women, at Aligarh Muslim University  and Shibli National College in Azamgarh.</p> <p><strong><a href="sites/default/files/Sugata%20Bose.pdf">The Rajendranath Das lecture in Bangla</a></strong></p> <p>The  Rajendranath Das lectureship on Bangla Studies, commencing in 2008, is a  part of the Berkeley Bangla Initiative, and was created by the  generosity of Satyen Das, is a lecture series that will bring a  prominent scholar of Bangla to speak at Berkeley annually.</p><p><strong><a href="http://southasia.berkeley.edu/tata-ises">Tata International Social Entrepreneurship Scheme</a></strong></p> <p>The Tata Group, one of India's largest private sector conglomerates and a global leader in innovative corporate social responsibility initiatives, in 2008 launched the Tata International Social Entrepreneurship Scheme (TISES). The primary objective of TISES is to provide international students with opportunities to contribute to community initiative projects of Tata Group companies in India and in so doing to promote international understanding. University of California Berkeley and Cambridge University in the UK are the first two participating universities. Berkeley will identify up to five upper division undergraduate or graduate students for 8-week summer TISES internships with Tata Group's community initiative programs. Through this program, competitively selected interns join Tata community development teams working on the economic and social empowerment of communities surrounding the company's operating units.</p>  </div>

  
  </div>
  </div>
</div>
  </div>
</div>

    <H3>Programs</H3>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><IMG src="http://vcro-vm-i002-dev08.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/shared/Kundan10red1.jpg" width=75 height=98></P>
<P>The Center for South Asia Studies has a wide range of programs that fall under three thematic areas: Contemporary South Asia, Culture and the Arts, and Community. We also have several privately funded programs and four endowed academic chairs. For more information about each of these programs, please click on the left menu bar.</P>  </div>

  <h2><a href="/rawmaintop" title=""></a></h2>

  <div class="meta">
  
    </div>

  <div class="content">

<div class="panel-region-separator"></div><div class="panel-pane pane-node-title"  id="page_title">
  
  
  
  <div class="pane-content">
    Study Abroad Programs  </div>

  
  </div>
<div class="panel-region-separator"></div><div class="panel-pane pane-node-body"  id="secondary_page_main">
  
  
  
  <div class="pane-content">
    <table border="0"><tbody><tr><td class="table_background" valign="top"><h3 style="text-align: right;"><span style="font-weight: normal; "> There are many ways to<br> incorporate India<br> into a rigorous program of<br> academic study - both at<br> the graduate and<br> undergraduate<br> levels</span></h3> <h3 style="text-align: right;"><span style="font-weight: normal;"><br>This is  a sample<br> of the many<br> programs available,<br> some of which are endorsed<br> by  UC Berkeley</span></h3> <h3 style="text-align: right;"><span style="font-weight: normal; "><br>Interested students<br> should investigate<br> programs of interest<br> to ensure<br> their particular needs<br> are met</span></h3></td><td><ul><li><a href="http://southasia.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/shared/2017_India_Winter_course_flyer.pdf" target="_blank">University of Iowa: Sustainable Development course in Kerala, India</a> - <strong>September 20, 2017 Deadline</strong></li><li style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.5em;"><a href="http://educationabroad.virginia.edu/" target="_blank">UVA in India</a> <strong>- November 1, 2017 deadline</strong></span></li><li style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.5em;"><a href="http://linglang.msu.edu/additional-programs/less-common-taught-languages/summer-online-language-courses/" target="_blank">MSU Summer Tamil Online Course</a><strong> - session 1 starts May 16; session 2 starts July 5</strong></span></li><li style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.5em;"><a href="https://southasia.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/shared/2018_language_flyers.pdf" target="_blank">AIIS Summer 2018 and Academic Year 2018-2019 Language Programs</a> - <strong>December 31, 2017<br></strong></span></li><li style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://sasli.wisc.edu/safli/" target="_blank">South Asian Flagship Languages Initiative (SAFLI) Boren Fellowship in Jaipur and Lucknow</a> - <strong>January 30, 2018</strong></li><li style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://sasli.wisc.edu/safli/" target="_blank">South Asian Flagship Languages Initiative (SAFLI) Boren Scholarship in Jaipur and Lucknow</a>&nbsp;-&nbsp;<strong style="font-size: 12px;">February 8, 2018</strong></li><li style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12px;"><a href="https://southasia.berkeley.edu/sites/default/files/shared/2018_NIRMAN_Programs_in_India-1.pdf" target="_blank">NIRMAN Programs in Varanasi, India<br></a></span></li><li style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://eap.ucop.edu/ourprograms/india/Pages/default.aspx?SRC=VURL&amp;KEY=India" target="_blank">UC Educational Abroad Programs in Delhi and Mumbai</a></li><li style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://studyabroad.berkeley.edu/" target="_blank">Berkeley Programs for Study Abroad</a></li></ul><ul><li><a href="http://www.acm.edu/off_campus_study/Apply_online.html" target="_blank">ACM India Studies Program (Associated Colleges of the Midwest)</a></li></ul><ul><li><a href="http://www.antioch.edu/aea/programs/buddhist-studies-in-india/" target="_blank">Antioch Education Abroad Buddhist Studies in India</a></li><li><a href="http://summerschool2017.chinfo.org/" target="_blank" style="background-color: #ffffff;">Chinmaya International Foundation Summer School Program&nbsp;</a></li><li><a href="http://www.sai.uni-heidelberg.de/sasweb/ausland/index_en.php">European Summer School on Modern South Asia [Heidelberg]</a></li><li><a href="http://www.indiastudyabroad.org/">India Study Abroad Center (ISAC)</a></li><li><a href="https://www.iesabroad.org/IES/Programs/India/india.html">Institute for the International Education of Students Study in India (IES)</a></li><li><a href="http://www.ihp.edu/page/rethinking_globalization/">International Honors Program Rethinking Globalization: Nature, Culture and Justice</a></li><li><a href="http://www.bowdoin.edu/isle/">Intercollegiate Sri Lanka Education (ISLE)</a>&nbsp;</li><li><a href="http://www.globalsemesters.com/India.html">Global Learning Semesters/Global Business Semesters</a></li><li><a href="https://studyabroad.rutgers.edu/index.cfm?FuseAction=Programs.MapSearch">Rutgers Study Abroad Study Abroad in India</a></li><li><a href="http://www.semesteratsea.org/">Semester at Sea</a></li><li><a href="http://sasli.wisc.edu/apply.html" style="background-color: #ffffff;">South Asian Summer Language Institute</a></li><li><a href="http://sitaprogram.org/">South India Term Abroad (SITA)</a></li><li><a href="http://www.sit.edu/" style="line-height: 18px; background-color: #ffffff;">School for International Training (SIT) Study Abroad</a></li><li><a href="http://www.umabroad.umn.edu/programs/ASIA/msidIndia/index.html">University of Minnesota Studies in International Development in India</a></li><li><a href="http://studyabroad.unc.edu/programs.cfm?pk=127">UNC Chapel Hill Study Abroad&nbsp;</a></li><li><a href="http://www.studyabroad.wisc.edu/programs/index.asp">University of Wisconsin Madison International Academic Programs in South Asia</a></li><li><a href="http://usac.unr.edu/study-abroad-programs/india">University Studies Abroad Consortium</a></li><li><a href="https://gcll.lums.edu.pk/summer" style="background-color: #ffffff;">Urdu Summer Program, Lahore</a><span style="font-size: 12px; background-color: #ffffff;">&nbsp;</span></li><li><span style="font-size: 12px; background-color: #ffffff;"><a href="http://cetacademicprograms.com/programs/india/uw-india/" style="background-color: #ffffff; text-decoration: underline;">UW in India</a><span style="font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.5em;"><a href="http://cetacademicprograms.com/programs/india/uw-india/">&nbsp;</a></span></span></li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table>  </div>
